[2023-04-05, 18:51:41] Deelaka Dias: import time
import os


# adding points to each driver after generate randomly
def add_points(driver_details, points):
    driver_details[4] = str(int(driver_details[4]) + points)
    return driver_details


# System should simulate a random race and assign pints to each driver accordingly.
def SRR():
    import random
    try:
        driver_file = open("Driver_details_Draft.txt", 'r')
        # checking if driver_file ia empty or not
        if os.path.getsize("Driver_details_Draft.txt") == 0:
            time.sleep(1.0)
            print("First you need enter driver details")
            time.sleep(0.5)
            print("You will direct to main menu")

        else:
            location_list = ["Nyirád", "Höljes", "Montalegre", "Barcelona", "Rīga", "Norway"]
            random_location = location_list[random.randint(0, 5)]

            import random
            year = random.randint(2010, 2023)
            month = random.randint(1, 12)
            month = str(month)
            if len(month) == 1:
                month = "0" + month
            day = random.randint(1, 28)
            day = str(day)
            if len(day) == 1:
                day = "0" + day
            Date = f"{year}-{month}-{day}"
            Date = str(Date)

            race_list_draft = []
            simulate = driver_file.readlines()
            driver_file.close()
            list_for_simulate = []

            for line in simulate:
                edit_line = line.strip().split(",")
                list_for_simulate.append(edit_line)
            if len(list_for_simulate) >= 3:

                random.shuffle(list_for_simulate)
                list_for_simulate[0] = add_points(list_for_simulate[0], 10)  # add points for 1st place
                list_for_simulate[1] = add_points(list_for_simulate[1], 7)  # add points for 2nd place
                list_for_simulate[2] = add_points(list_for_simulate[2], 5)  # add points for 3rd place

                x = f"{'Position':15s}{'Name':30s}{'Team':30s}{'Points':5s}"

                position_1 = f"{str(1):15s}{(list_for_simulate[0][0]):30s}{(list_for_simulate[0][2]):30s}{str(list_for_simulate[0][4]):5s}"

                position_2 = f"{str(2):15s}{(list_for_simulate[1][0]):30s}{(list_for_simulate[1][2]):30s}{str(list_for_simulate[1][4]):5s}"

                position_3 = f"{str(3):15s}{(list_for_simulate[2][0]):30s}{(list_for_simulate[2][2]):30s}{str(list_for_simulate[2][4]):5s}"

                driver_file_1 = open("Random_Race.txt", 'a', encoding='utf-16')
                # opening the race_file in utf-16 because it contains unicodes
                driver_file_1.write("Location: ")
                driver_file_1.write(random_location+'\t\t')
                driver_file_1.write("Date: ")
                driver_file_1.write(Date+'\n \n')
                driver_file_1.write(x + '\n')
                driver_file = open("Driver_details_Draft.txt", 'w')

                for line in range(0,len(list_for_simulate)):
                    driver_file.write(",".join(list_for_simulate[line]) + "\n")
                driver_file.close()
                driver_file_1.write(position_1 + '\n')
                driver_file_1.write(position_2 + '\n')
                driver_file_1.write(position_3 + '\n')

                for j in range(3,len(list_for_simulate)):
                    position_n = f"{str(j+1):15s}{(list_for_simulate[j][0]):30s}{(list_for_simulate[j][2]):30s}{str(list_for_simulate[j][4]):5s}"
                    driver_file_1.write(position_n + "\n")

                race_file = open("Race_List.txt", 'a', encoding='utf-16')
                race_list_draft.append(random_location)
                race_list_draft.append(Date)
                driver_file_1.write("\n")
                driver_file_1.write("\n")
                race_file.write(",".join(race_list_draft) + "\n")
                race_file.close()
                driver_file_1.close()
                race_list_draft.clear()
                #time.sleep(0.5)
                print("Races were generated randomly, look for the Random Race file")
                #time.sleep(1.5)

            else:
                time.sleep(0.1)
                print("You have to enter at least 3 driver details to perform SRR")
                time.sleep(1.0)
                print("You will jump to the main program")
            time.sleep(0.5)
    except FileNotFoundError:
        time.sleep(0.5)
        print("First you need to execute STF")
        time.sleep(0.5)
        print("You will direct to main menu")
        time.sleep(1.0)

[2023-09-22, 07:19:32] Arkhash IIT: package com.example.demo;

import javafx.fxml.FXML;
import javafx.scene.control.Label;
import javafx.application.Platform;

public class HelloController {
    @FXML
    private Label welcomeText;

    @FXML
    protected void onHelloButtonClick() {
        Thread countdownThread = new Thread(new Runnable() {
            @Override
            public void run() {
                for (int i = 0; i > -4000; i--) {
                    final int val = i;
                    Platform.runLater(new Runnable() {
                        @Override
                        public void run() {
                            updateLabel(val);
                        }
                    });
                    try {
                        Thread.sleep(1000);
                    } catch (InterruptedException e) {
                        System.out.println(e);
                    }
                }
            }
        });
        countdownThread.start();
    }

    private void updateLabel(int val) {
        welcomeText.setText(String.valueOf(val));
    }
}

[2023-11-18, 18:43:55] Arkhash IIT: public void displayAdmissionNumError() {
    if (Student.admissionNumStatus.equals("empty")) {
        studentRegisterAdmissionNumErrorLabel.setText("Admission Number cannot be empty.");
    } else if (Student.admissionNumStatus.equals("format")) {
        studentRegisterAdmissionNumErrorLabel.setText("Admission number should contain only numeric values.");
    } else if (Student.admissionNumStatus.equals("length")) {
        studentRegisterAdmissionNumErrorLabel.setText("Admission Number has to be 4 digits.");
    } else if (Student.admissionNumStatus.equals("exist")) {
        studentRegisterAdmissionNumErrorLabel.setText("Admission Number already exists.");
    } else {
        studentRegisterAdmissionNumErrorLabel.setText("");
    }
}

[2023-12-06, 22:51:28] Arkhash IIT: def depth_first_search(start, goal):
    # Initialize Frontier with the start cell
    frontier = [start]
    
    # Initialize Explored set
    explored = set()
    
    # Perform depth-first search
    while frontier:
        # Pop the current cell from the Frontier
        curr_cell = frontier.pop()
        
        # Check if the goal is reached
        if curr_cell == goal:
            print("Goal reached!")
            return True
        
        # Explore neighbors in the order of W > N > S > E
        for direction in ['W', 'N', 'S', 'E']:
            # Calculate the child cell based on the direction
            child_cell = get_child_cell(curr_cell, direction)
            
            # Check if the child cell is already explored
            if child_cell in explored:
                continue
            
            # Add child cell to both Explored and Frontier
            explored.add(child_cell)
            frontier.append(child_cell)
    
    # If the loop completes and goal is not reached, return False
    print("Goal not reached.")
    return False

def get_child_cell(curr_cell, direction):
    # Implement logic to calculate the child cell based on the current cell and direction
    # This depends on the structure of your grid or graph
    # You may need to adjust this function accordingly
    # Example: For a 2D grid, you might update the coordinates based on the direction
    pass

# Example usage:
start_cell = (0, 0)  # Replace with the actual start cell
goal_cell = (5, 5)   # Replace with the actual goal cell

depth_first_search(start_cell, goal_cell)

import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

def logistic_function(x):
    return 1 / (1 + np.exp(-x))

# Generate x values
x_values = np.linspace(-6, 6, 100)  # Adjust the range as needed

# Calculate corresponding y values
y_values = logistic_function(x_values)

# Plot the logistic function
plt.plot(x_values, y_values, label='Logistic Function')
plt.title('Logistic Function')
plt.xlabel('x')
plt.ylabel('f(x)')
plt.legend()
plt.grid(True)
plt.show()
[2023-12-12, 17:49:14] Deelaka Dias: # part b

import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

def logistic_function(x):
    return 1 / (1 + np.exp(-x))

def logistic_derivative(x):
    f_x = logistic_function(x)
    return f_x * (1 - f_x)

# Generate x values
x_values = np.linspace(-6, 6, 100)  # Adjust the range as needed

# Calculate corresponding y values for the derivative
y_derivative_values = logistic_derivative(x_values)

# Plot the derivative of the logistic function
plt.plot(x_values, y_derivative_values, label="Derivative of Logistic Function")
plt.title('Derivative of Logistic Function')
plt.xlabel('x')
plt.ylabel("f'(x)")
plt.legend()
plt.grid(True)
plt.show()

import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

# Define the function
def function_to_plot(x):
    return np.tan(np.sin(3*x)**2)

# Generate x values
x_values = np.linspace(-2*np.pi, 2*np.pi, 400)  # Adjust the range as needed

# Calculate corresponding y values
y_values = function_to_plot(x_values)

# Plot the function
plt.plot(x_values, y_values, label=r'$\tan(\sin^2(3x))$')
plt.title('Plot of tan(sin^2(3x))')
plt.xlabel('x')
plt.ylabel('y')
plt.legend()
plt.grid(True)
plt.show()

import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

# Define the function
def function_to_plot(x):
    return -x**4 + 2*x**2 - 0.5*x + 10

# Generate x values
x_values = np.linspace(-3, 3, 400)  # Adjust the range as needed

# Calculate corresponding y values
y_values = function_to_plot(x_values)

# Plot the function
plt.plot(x_values, y_values, label=r'$-x^4 + 2x^2 - 0.5x + 10$')
plt.title('Plot of -x^4 + 2x^2 - 0.5x + 10')
plt.xlabel('x')

plt.legend()

import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

# Define the function
def function_to_plot(x):
    return np.exp(-x * np.log(x**2))

# Generate x values (avoiding x <= 0 to prevent undefined values for ln(x))
x_values = np.linspace(0.01, 3, 400)

# Calculate corresponding y values
y_values = function_to_plot(x_values)

# Plot the function
plt.plot(x_values, y_values, label=r'$e^{-x \ln(x^2)}$')
plt.title('Plot of $e^{-x \ln(x^2)}$')
plt.xlabel('x')
plt.ylabel('y')
plt.legend()
plt.grid(True)
plt.show()

import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

# Define the function
def function_to_plot(x):
    return x**2 * np.sin(np.sin(3*x)) - 3 * np.cos(np.cos(2*x - np.pi/3))

# Generate x values
x_values = np.linspace(-5, 5, 400)  # Adjust the range as needed

# Calculate corresponding y values
y_values = function_to_plot(x_values)

# Plot the function
plt.plot(x_values, y_values, label=r'$x^2 \sin(\sin(3x)) - 3\cos(\cos(2x - \frac{\pi}{3}))$')
plt.title('Plot of $x^2 \sin(\sin(3x)) - 3\cos(\cos(2x - \frac{\pi}{3}))$')
plt.xlabel('x')
plt.ylabel('y')
plt.legend()
plt.grid(True)
plt.show()
[2023-12-12, 17:50:05] Deelaka Dias: #  part d

import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

# Define the original function
def original_function(x):
    return x**2 * np.sin(np.sin(3*x)) - 3 * np.cos(np.cos(2*x - np.pi/3))

# Define the logistic function
def logistic_function(x):
    return 1 / (1 + np.exp(-x))

# Apply logistic function to the original function
def transformed_function(x):
    return logistic_function(original_function(x))

# Generate x values
x_values = np.linspace(-5, 5, 400)

# Calculate corresponding y values for the transformed function
y_values_transformed = transformed_function(x_values)

# Plot the original and transformed functions
plt.figure(figsize=(10, 6))

plt.subplot(2, 1, 1)
plt.plot(x_values, original_function(x_values), label='Original Function')
plt.title('Original Function')
plt.xlabel('x')
plt.ylabel('y')
plt.legend()
plt.grid(True)

plt.subplot(2, 1, 2)
plt.plot(x_values, y_values_transformed, label='Transformed Function')
plt.title('Logistic Function Applied')
plt.xlabel('x')
plt.ylabel('y')
plt.legend()
plt.grid(True)

plt.tight_layout()
plt.show()

# part a 

import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

#fuction 
def f(x):
    return x*np.sin(x/4)

# plotting the function 
x = np.linspace(-6*np.pi, 3*np.pi, 100)
y = f(x)

# Plot the function

plt.plot(x, y)
plt.title('Graph of $f(x) $')
plt.xlabel('$x$')
plt.ylabel('$f(x)$')
plt.show()


# part b

# the x variable is defined 
x = sp.symbols('x')
# the function is defined for sin(x)
function_x = sp.sin(x)

# the taylor series is evaluated at x=pi/4 for the first 10 terms
taylor_series_vals = sp.series(function_x, x, sp.pi/4, 20).removeO()

# print the first 10 terms in the series
taylor_series_vals



# part c

func_x = sp.sin(x)
t_series = sp.series(func_x, x, sp.pi/4, 50).removeO()

# Convert the symbolic expression to a numerical function
taylor_fn = sp.lambdify(x, t_series, 'numpy')

# Generate x values for the plot
x_val = np.linspace(-6*np.pi, 3*np.pi, 1000)

# Generate y values using the Taylor series function
y_val = taylor_fn(x_val)

# Generate y values for the original function
y_values_original = np.sin(x_val)

# Plot the results
plt.figure(figsize=(8, 8))
plt.plot(x_val, y_val, label=r'$\sin x$', linewidth=2)
plt.plot(x_val, y_val, label='Taylor Series (50 terms)')
plt.title('Taylor Series of $\\sin x$ when $x = \\frac{\pi}{4}$')
plt.xlabel('x-vals')
plt.ylabel('y-vals')
plt.axhline(0, color='green',linewidth=0.6)
plt.axvline(0, color='green',linewidth=0.6)
plt.legend()
plt.grid(color='blue', linestyle='-', linewidth=0.6)
plt.show()



# part d 

estimation = taylor_fn(np.pi/4)
actual_value = (np.pi / 2) * np.sin(np.pi / 4)


change = estimation - actual_value
variation = np.absolute(change)

print('The difference is: ', variation)

[2023-12-16, 09:08:37] Arkhash IIT: def fourier_series(x, n):
    a0 = integrate.quad(f, -np.pi, np.pi)[0] / (2 * np.pi)
    result = np.zeros_like(x)
    for i in range(1, n+1):
        an = (1/np.pi) * integrate.quad(lambda x: f(x) * np.cos(i*x), -np.pi, np.pi)[0]
        bn = (1/np.pi) * integrate.quad(lambda x: f(x) * np.sin(i*x), -np.pi, np.pi)[0]
        result += an * np.cos(i*x) + bn * np.sin(i*x)
    return a0/2 + result

# Choose the number of terms in the Fourier series
num_terms = 10

# Calculate the Fourier series expansion
series_expansion = fourier_series(x, num_terms)

from scipy.fftpack import dct, idct
from matplotlib import pyplot as plt
from scipy import integrate

# Placeholder functions (replace with actual implementations)
def custom_block_dct(block):
    return dct(dct(block.T, norm='ortho').T, norm='ortho')

def custom_resize_image_dct(image, size):
    # Replace with your image resizing logic
    return image

def custom_quantize_block(block, custom_Q):
    return np.round(block / custom_Q)

def custom_dequantize_block(block, custom_Q):
    return block * custom_Q

def custom_compress_image_dct(image, custom_Q):
    rows, cols = image.shape
    compressed_image = np.zeros_like(image, dtype=float)

    for i in range(0, rows, 8):
        for j in range(0, cols, 8):
            block = image[i:i+8, j:j+8]
            dct_block = custom_block_dct(block)
            quantized_block = custom_quantize_block(dct_block, custom_Q)
            compressed_image[i:i+8, j:j+8] = custom_dequantize_block(quantized_block, custom_Q)

    compressed_image = np.clip(compressed_image, 0, 255)
    compressed_image = compressed_image.astype(np.uint8)

    return compressed_image

# Example usage
custom_Q = 20
custom_resized_image = custom_resize_image_dct(image_array, (240, 240))
custom_compressed_image = custom_compress_image_dct(custom_resized_image, custom_Q)

# Visualize the original, resized, and compressed image
plt.subplot(311), plt.imshow(image_array, cmap='gray')
plt.title('Original Image'), plt.xticks([]), plt.yticks([])

plt.subplot(312), plt.imshow(custom_resized_image, cmap='gray')
plt.title('Resized Image (240x240)'), plt.xticks([]), plt.yticks([])

plt.subplot(313), plt.imshow(custom_compressed_image, cmap='gray')
plt.title(f'Compressed Image (Q={custom_Q})'), plt.xticks([]), plt.yticks([])

plt.show()
